A bohemian area nestled in the middle of Rome, this area inspires a luring energy of mystique to those lucky enough to enter the realms of this gem. Perfectly blending ancient and contemporary, wandering the cobblestone streets will have you weaving in and out of effortlessly cool boutiques, vintage bookstores and chic cafes. Socializing around Piazza della Madonna dei Monti in the center of town, the energy levels always remain high without ever feeling too crowded. Once you have had your fill of people-watching at the piazza, head over to Ai Tre Scalini for a glass of their fabulous house wine and intimate ambiance. With the charming yet relaxing atmosphere, there can never be too much time spent in Monti as it will surely have you reconsidering your current permanent residence.
